**GT simplified form:**

```
96.829*epsilon*(-0.00975*(T - 352.18) + 1) - 0.4784*(T - 352.18) + 8.062*(T - 352.18)*log(epsilon + 1)
```

Expanding:
- `96.829*epsilon*(-0.00975*T + 0.00975*352.18 + 1)` = `96.829*epsilon*(-0.00975*T + 3.4338 + 1)` = `96.829*epsilon*(-0.00975*T + 4.4338)`
- = `-0.9443*T*epsilon + 429.33*epsilon`

- `8.062*(T - 352.18)*log(epsilon + 1)` = `8.062*T*log(epsilon+1) - 2839.3*log(epsilon+1)`

So GT = **-0.9443*T*epsilon + 429.33*epsilon - 0.4784*T + 168.52 + 8.062*T*log(epsilon+1) - 2839.3*log(epsilon+1)**

This has terms: `T*epsilon`, `epsilon`, `T`, constant, `T*log(epsilon+1)`, `log(epsilon+1)`

Now I need to find a candidate that can produce all these terms.

**Candidate 47:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + c2*epsilon/(c3 + epsilon) + c4*epsilon**c5*log(c6*epsilon + 1)`

This has `T*epsilon`, `T`, but `epsilon/(c3+epsilon)` instead of `epsilon`, and `epsilon^c5*log(...)` which can give `epsilon*log(epsilon+1)` but not `T*log(epsilon+1)`. No match.

**Candidate 57:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*epsilon**3 + c5*epsilon*log(c6*epsilon + 1)`

**Candidate 3:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*epsilon**3 + c5*epsilon + c6*log(c7*epsilon + 1)`

Has `T`, `T*epsilon`, `epsilon`, `log(epsilon+1)`, but no `T*log(epsilon+1)`. Missing.

**Candidate 14:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*epsilon**3 + c5*exp(T*c6)*log(c7*epsilon + 1)`
